## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy Admin API Endpoint Registration

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement the admin API: the admin handler registration (addHandler), the /clusters, /listeners, /config_dump, and /stats endpoint implementations, and the admin filter chain setup.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

The answer file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Summary of Envoy Admin API Endpoint Registration

### Architecture Overview

The Envoy admin API is implemented in `source/server/admin/` with a clean separation of concerns:

1. **Interface** (`envoy/server/admin.h`): Defines the `Admin` abstract class with `addHandler()`, `addStreamingHandler()`, `removeHandler()`, `makeRequest()`, and the `MAKE_ADMIN_HANDLER` macro.

2. **Core Implementation** (`source/server/admin/admin.cc` + `admin.h`): `AdminImpl` class that:
   - Registers all built-in handlers in its constructor (lines 126–260 of `admin.cc`)
   - Implements `addHandler()` / `addStreamingHandler()` for dynamic handler registration
   - Sets up the **admin filter chain** via `createFilterChain()` (adds `AdminFilter` HTTP stream filter) and `createNetworkFilterChain()` (adds `ConnectionManagerImpl`)
   - Routes requests via `makeRequest()` using linear prefix-matching
   - Contains inner classes `AdminFilterChain`, `AdminListener`, `AdminListenSocketFactory`

3. **Admin Filter** (`admin_filter.cc/h`): `AdminFilter` is the terminal HTTP stream decoder filter that dispatches requests to handlers via `AdminFilter::onComplete()`.

4. **Endpoint Handlers**:
   - `/clusters` → `ClustersHandler::handlerClusters()` in `clusters_handler.cc`
   - `/listeners` → `ListenersHandler::handlerListenerInfo()` in `listeners_handler.cc`
   - `/config_dump` → `ConfigDumpHandler::handlerConfigDump()` in `config_dump_handler.cc`
   - `/stats` → `StatsHandler::makeRequest()` in `stats_handler.cc`
   - Plus handlers for `/logging`, `/runtime`, `/server_info`, `/healthcheck`, `/cpuprofiler`, etc.

5. **Config Validation Stub** (`source/server/config_validation/admin.cc/h`): `ValidationAdmin`
